Data on encounter histories, growth and clutch sizes of mature female snapping turtles in Algonquin Park, Canada, from 1972-2012.

list(

# PART A: DATA ON VITAL RATES, ABUNDANCE AND RECRUITMENT TO END OF STUDY

year.start = 1972,	# first year of data
n.years=41,		# no. years of data (1972-2012)
M.obs=223,		# no. mature females observed in North Madawaska River catchment (NMRC) from 1972-2012
M=263,			# no. NMRC 1972-2012 females, incl. 40 hypothetical females added through data augmentation
n.ind.growth=377,  	# total females in 1972-2012 data set, including 114 from outside NMRC
			# these 114 females provided additional data on growth and clutch sizes

matmed=17,		# median (and mean) age at maturity
matmin=11,		# minimum age at maturity
matk=15,		# number of different ages at which females may mature
# Multinomial probabilities for maturing at each of those different ages, i.e., 11 to 25 years
pmat=c(0.01,0.02,0.05,0.08,0.12,0.15,0.15,0.13,0.1,0.07,0.05,0.03,0.02,0.01,0.01),

alpha.site=c(1,1,1),	# uniform probability of being at Sasajewun Lake, Amoyoa Swamp, or other site
